# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 00:30:27.892020

### Base Program

```py
def min_steps(n):
    result = 0
    i = 2
    while i <= n:
        while n % i == 0:
            result += i
            n //= i
        i += 1
    return result
```

### Input

```json
[83]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def min_steps(n):
    result = 0
    i = 2
    while i <= n:
        while n % i == 0:
            result += i
            n //= i
        i += 1
    return result
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def min_steps(var_0):
    result = 0
    i = 2
    while i <= var_0:
        while var_0 % i == 0:
            result += i
            var_0 //= i
        i += 1
    return result
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def min_steps(var_1):
    result = 0
    i = 2
    while i <= var_1:
        while var_1 % i == 0:
            result += i
            var_1 //= i
        i += 1
    return result
```
